Quant tu cures la maladie de la mice de ceu que nos avons dit as divisions des cures, et il ne profite mie, adonques i afierent III manieres de cautere que tuit sont boin.	When you treat the mouse disease that we have said about divisions of treatment, and it does not improve, then they resort to three methods of fire cauterization that are all good.
Desquelz li une maniere si est que tu faices III cauteres, ou IIII, en lignant selonc la longor de la mice, selonc la figure dou cautere dou foie que nos avons dit devant; et n’apresser mie ta main a tout le cautere, et soit li malaides sovins sor son dos; et une autre maniere de cautere si est que tu eschaufe le cautere qui a II ners, si com nos l’avons mostreit en la dislocation de l’espaule; et lieve le keur qui est endroit la mice, ou li coutes dou malaide vient devers senestre, et soit li elevations dont tu lieves le keur selonc la keur, selonc la longesce dou cors, et li cautere soient selonc la largesce dou cors.	When there is a way that you make three or four cauteries, lining them along the length of the wound, according to the shape of the liver cauteries we have mentioned before; and do not press your hand on the entire cautery, and let the hairs be on its back; and another way of cauterizing is that you heat the cauterizer with two needles, as we have shown in the dislocation of the shoulder; and lift the curtain that is near the wound, or the ear where the pain of the hair comes from the right side, and let the elevations that you lift the curtain according to its curve, according to the length of the body, and the cauterizer should be according to the width of the body.
Aprés i boute les II ners enflamez tant que li keurs soit perciez de l’autre part, et puis trai fuers le cautere, et ensi en i avra IIII Et se tu vues, si cauterize a tot le cautere a III ners.	After boiling the two needles until they are perceived to be hot from the other side, then remove the caustic, and thus enter one inch, and if you see, then cauterize with the entire caustic at three needles.
Aprés le cure quant il a geteit porriture par lonc tens, et ce vaut mues que li autre des cures devant dites.	After the treatment when it has grown worse due to prolonged tension, and this is appropriate that the other cures before mentioned should be done.
de ydropisie	of hydropsy
Cautere ne vaut a ydropique, fors c’a la maniere qui est apelee «asclytes».	Caustic is not good for hydropsy, except in the manner which is called "asclepiades".
Quant tu la cures selonc les manieres que nos avons dit en divisions, et ta cure ne profite mie, adonques covient il que tu li faices IIII cauteres entor la boude, et I sus l’estomac, et un sus le foie, et I sus la mice, et II derrier le dos sus l’espinee, et I endroit le pis; et soit li cauteres bien pres de l’espés dou keur.	When you treat it according to the methods that we have said in divisions, and your treatment does not help, then it is necessary that you make four cauteries around the belly, and one above the stomach, and one above the liver, and one above the spleen, and one behind the back on the spine, and one at the worst place; and let the cauteries be close to the part which is affected.
Aprés laisse le cautere aovert por giter porriture lonc tens, et ne lassier mie la cure dou malaide aprés le cautere; et sanation se hasterait, et seront ensamble les II ententions avec l’aide de Deu.	After leaving the fire cauterizer for a while to cool down long and tight, and not letting go of the care of the pain after the cauterization; and healing would hasten, and together with the help of God, the two intentions would be fulfilled.
Li forme dou cautere por le ventre soit li clavile que nos avons devant mostreit; et cil por le dos soit olivaire, selonc ceu qu’il est ci devant mis.	The shape of the fire cauterizer for the belly is like the one we have shown before; and for the back, it is an olive branch, as it is written above.
de l’enfleure des piez	of the swelling of the feet
Quant li piez sont enflez a celui qui est ydropique, et sont plain d’awe citrine, il covient que tu cauterizes sus le dos dou piet entre l’auriculaire et l’anulaire; et lieve ta main avec le cautere sens torner.	When the feet are swollen in someone who is hydroptic, and they are plain of yellow bile, it is necessary to cauterize above the foot between the auricular and the annular; and let your hand with the cauterizer towards returning.
Et n’entrer mie trop em parfont, ensi sarrait fuers li awe citrine, et soit li cauteres selonc cest forme:	And do not enter too deeply into the flesh, thus avoiding the yellowish part, and let the cauteries be done in this form:
Aprés fai sus II jambes II cauteres en chescune jambe a la pointe dou cutellaire; et soit li cauteres dou lonc, l’un desoz le genoil devant et l’autre defuers, enmi la jambe; et laisse les cauteres aovers longement sens curer, que li awe en isse; aprés le cure des autres cures que nos avons dit.	After making incisions above the two legs, apply two cauteries in each leg at the tip of a sharp knife; and let the cauteries be long, one on the side in front and the other behind, in the leg; and leave the cauteries hanging for a long time to cure the wound that is in it.
de la menoison	of the menstruation
Quant solution de ventre vient de froidor et de moistor, tant que li vertus retentive et digestive qui est ou stomac et en l’intestine est afleboie, et ne puet estre curez par manieres de cures; et tu vois le malaide bien soffrant et de fort vertut, si fai I grant cautere sus l’estomac selonc ceu qu’il en a parleit ci devant ou cautere de l’estomac, au cautere circule; et IIII cauteres entor la boude subtilz a tout I cautere clavile subtil, et II cauteres sus les hainches.	When the solution of the belly comes from cold and moisture, as long as the retentive and digestive virtues that are in the stomach and in the intestines are blocked, and cannot be cured by any means of cures; and you see the pain is very great and of great virtue, then make a great cauterization above the stomach according to what he has spoken before or a cauterization of the stomach, with the cauterization circulating; and four cauterizations around the belly, all the time, and two cauterizations on the hips.
Et se tu vois les moistors habundans et le malaide soffrant, se li fai cautere sus le poignil, et I cautere sus chaicun yle, et II petis cauteres sus l’estomac delez le grant, car li cure est profitans quant il i a bone aide.	If you see abundant moisture and the pain is intense, then perform fire cauterization on the base of the nail, and I cauterize each one, and II small cauterizations above the stomach below the large one, for the cure is beneficial when it has good help.
de la cure des emorroydes	of the treatment of wart
Quant les emorroydes sont ou fondement, ou une ou plusors, et sont ancienes et sont de grosses humors froides et moistes corrumpues, et sont curees si com nos avons dit en divisions, et il ne profite mie, si fai cauteres: III sus l’espine dou dos, celi qui est tout defuers desoz almecdate poc et poc en triangulant, et I cautere desoz la boude II dois; et se tu penses que ses estomac soit refroidiez, et li viande ne cuise, et on voit enfler la faice, adonques li faice on I grant cautere sus le stomac, si com il est devant dit, et I autre sus le foie, et I autre sus la mice a tout le cautere clavile; et laisse le cautere overt lonc tens.	When the warts are on the foundation, or one or more, and are old and are large humors cold and moist corrupted, and are cured as we have said in divisions, and it does not improve, then perform cauterizations: III above the spine of the back, which is all before unmelted little by little in triangular, and I cauterization outside the belly II doses; and if you think that his stomach is cooled, and the food does not cook, and one sees the face swells, then the face has I large cauterization above the stomach, as it was previously said, and I other above the liver, and I other above the mouse at all the cauterization clavile; and leave the cauterization open long ten.
Aprés cure le leu tant qu’il soit sanez.	After healing, the limb as long as it is healthy.
de la charnositeit qui est nommee «thelul»	of the cartilage that is called "thelul
Quant tu copes althelul, si eschaufe le cautere qui semble I raseur, et puis le met tout embraseit sus cel althelul copeit; et i laisse tant ta main que li cauteres viegne a la naissance de la voine, de coi li sans cort; fai ceu une fois ou II, et s’il i a mout d’althelul, si cauterize chaicun si com nos avons dit; aprés les cure d’oignemens profitans tant qu’il soient sanez; et se tu cauterizes d’un cautere grant sus alchatim, si avra plus grant aide.	When you cut into the cartilage, if the fire cauterizes as if it were a razor, and then put it all on fire above the cartilage cut; and let your hand so that the cauterizer comes to the opening of the vein, from which the bleeding stops; do this once or twice, and if there is much cartilage, cauterize each one as we have said; after curing wounds benefiting as long as they are healthy; and if you cauterize with a large fire above the cartilage, it will have greater help.
de plaie mal curee	of an improperly treated wound
Quant li malaides ne puet soffrir tailleure ne overture, que nos raconterons en son leu, si vient teil maladie que ne puet estre sanee fuer que par cautere.	When the wound cannot be suffered by a lancer or opened, as we will tell you in its place, if it is an illness that cannot be healed except by cauterization.
Quant a aucun vient fistule, et est enveillie et giete porriture et moistors corrumpues, si la doies prover a tot une tente subtil, et garde que tu saiches a tot la tente combien elle a de parfont.	When any comes with fistula, and is awake and given porridge and corrupted moisture, then you must apply a thin tent to all of it, and guard that you wash the tent as much as it has of purity.
Aprés eschaufe le cautere qui semble I raseur, et le boute en la fistule selonc la quantiteit que li tente i est entrée, et rencomence lou cautere tant que cil cors porris et corrumpus soient ars, une fois, ou II ou III, selonc la quantiteit de som besoing; et te warde d’ardre lé nerf qui sunt enqui, et des grans voinnes.	After heating the cauterizer which seems like a razor, and put it into the fistula according to the amount that the tent has entered, and continue the cauterization until the wound is cleansed and corrupted are burned away, once, or twice, or three times, according to the amount of need; and guard against burning the nerves which are near, and great veins.
se li fistule vait au cors de la vesie et a l’intestine, si te warde de ces leus, et ne faire ceu fuers que en leu charnut, et pense qu’ele n’est mie persans; aprés cure le leu tant qu’il soit sanez, et se li leus est saielez, et les matieres sont ostees lonc tens, adonc saiches que li leus est sanez entierement; et se les matieres ne sont ostees, saiche que li leus est troez, et corrumpus li os au font; et ensi com un de ces que nos dirons en son leu.	If the fistula goes to the core of the bladder and the intestine, you should avoid these things, and only do what is necessary in the meantime, and think that it is not yet healed; after curing the wound as long as it is healthy, and if the wound is not clean, and the matter is removed along with the tenacity, then wash the wound so that it is completely healed; and if the matter is not removed, wash the wound so that it is torn, and corrode the bone at the source; and thus like one of these that we will say in its wound.
de la maladie des reins	of the disease of the kidneys
Quant dolor de froit vient as rains, et de grosse ventositeit, et ne prent talant de femme, adonc covient il que tu li fais cautere sus les rains d’une part et d’autre au cautere clavile que nos avons devant dit; et se nos le cauterizons em mileu, si avra III cauteres en ligne, et se feront plus grant aide.	When pain from frost comes to rain, and with great moisture, and does not take the form of a woman, then it is necessary that you make fire cauterization on the rains from both sides at the clavile cautery that we have already mentioned; and if we cauterize in the middle, there will be three cauterizations in a line, and they will be greater help.
de la vessie	of the bladder
Quant li vessie est mole et foible de froit et de moistor, si que li malaides retient l’urine, adonc li fai cautere en la partie defuers sus la vessie, la ou encomencent li poil dou poignil, et I a destre et I a senestre, et soit chescuns cauteres si lons com li nous d’un poce; et li fais I cautere defuers le dos, ou II se tu en as besoing; et soit li cauteres clavile selon la forme devant dite.	When the bladder is small and weak from frost and moisture, and if the pain retains urine, then make fire cauterization in the part before the bladder, where the hair begins to grow on both sides, and each cauterization should be as long as a finger; and make one cauterization behind the back, or two if you have need; and let the clavile cauterization be done according to the form previously mentioned.
de la marris	of the marsh
Quant li marrix est froide et moiste, et ne laisse mie por ceu a concevoir, et les flors sont corrumpues et lor termines tarde; et quant elles vienent, si sent grant dolor: adonques covient il c’on li faice III cauteres entor la boude, si com nos avons dit ou cautere de la vessie, et II cauteres defuers le dos; et soit li cauteres clavile, si com nos avons dit.	When the marsh is cold and wet, and does not allow for conception, and the flowers are corrupted and their terms are late; and when they come, it causes great pain: therefore, it is necessary to do three cauteries around the abdomen, as we have said of the cautery of the bladder, and two cauteries before the back; and let the cauteries be sharp, as we have said.
de la hainche	of the belly
Quant les moistors viscouses dessendent a la boiste de la hainche, et por ceste cause si se muet de son leu, et li signes est que li cuisse est plus longe que li autre quant on le mesure ensamble; et est trovez li leus dou departement vuis, si covient que tu cauterizes le malaide sus la boiste de la hainche a I cautere semblant au cercle, et seigne devant le leu entor la boiste si com elle torne, si que li boiste soit dedens le cercle; et si soit li cauteres telz com cil dont on a cauterizeit le stomac.	When viscous moisture descends to the belly button, and for this reason it moves out of its place, and the signs are that one thigh is longer than the other when measured together; and it is found that the eyes are displaced, then it is necessary to cauterize the pain above the belly button with a cautery similar to a circle, and sign before the skin around the belly button as it turns, so that the belly is inside the circle; and if it is such cauteries as those which have been cauterized in the stomach.
Et se cist cauteres ne t’est presens, se li fai III cauteres de l’olivaire grans, et soit li cauteres ausi parfont com tous li keurs; et le cure tant qu’il soit sanez.	And if this fire cautery is not present, make three large olive oil burns as cauteries, and treat them all equally; and let the wound heal.
de la dolor de la hainche	of the pain in the back
Quant dolor vient en la boiste de la hainche, et c’est de froidor et de moistor, et li malaides est curez de ceu que nos avons dit en la division et li cure ne vaut, et li maladie est anciene: adonc covient il que tu purges le malaide des grosses humors de pilules fetides, ou autres pilules bones semblans.	When pain comes in the back of the chest, and it is from cold and moisture, and the hairs are cured of what we have said in the division and the treatment does not work, and the disease is old: therefore, it is necessary to purge the hair of large humors with fetid pills or other good-quality pills.
Aprés li fai cautere; et li maniere dou cautere si est selonc II manieres: c’est a savoir ensamble medicines ardans, et cautere de feu.	After doing the cauterization; and the method of the cauterization is as follows: that is to say, together with burning medicines, and fire cauterization.
Cautere de feu si est selonc mout de manieres, desquelz li uns est telz: que tu cauterize sus la boiste de la hainche III cauteres triangulalz selonc ceste forme, et i fai bone profunditeit et grant, et ait entre chaicun cautere d’espaice la groissece d’un doi, et soit li cauteres olivaire; aucune fois fait on cautere en mileu sus lou chief de la hainche, por coi il en i a IIII selonc ceste forme:	Fire cauterization is performed in many ways, such as: you cauterize above the ribs of the back three triangular cauterizations in this form, and make good depth and great, and there should be between each cauterization a space of the size of one, and let the cauterizing oil; never make a cauterization in the middle above the back, because it has four in this form:
Et se tu vues, si le cauterize au cautere dou cercle que nos avons devant dit en la dislocation de la hainche; mais fai en teil maniere que li cercles conteigne toute la hainche, et tous li espés dou keur soit ars.	And if you see, if the cauterization is made with the circle that we have previously mentioned in the dislocation of the back; but make it in a different way so that the circles contain the whole back, and all the sharp points should be rounded.
Et c’est li maniere c’on fait en sciatique, quant li dolor tient en la hainche, et ne parvient mie jusc’a la cuisse ne jusc’a la jambe.	And this is the way it is done in lithotomy, when the pain is in the groin and does not reach up to the thigh or the leg.
Et s’ele vient jusc’a la cuisse et la jambe, se li fai II cauteres lai ou li malaides dit que li dolor li tient, et I cautere desus la cheville IIII dois, a la partie senestre un poc; et soit li cauteres cutellaire, et soit arse li espesseté dou keur; et se li malaides sent que li dolor s’estende jusc’a dois dou piet ou pres d’enqui, se le cauterize la ou il sent la dolor III poins ou IIII au cautere qui est apelez «poins».	And if it comes up to the thigh and the leg, then two cautery irons are applied where the pain is, and one cautery iron four times, at the part on the right side; and let the cautery irons be sharp, and let the thickness of the cautery be as thin as possible; and if the patient feels that the pain extends to two fingers or near the ankle, then cauterize where he feels the pain three times or four with the cautery iron called "poins".
Et se mestiers est, se li en fai plus; et se il seit que li dolor soit desoz le genoil vers la cuisse, se li fais cautere au cautere cutellaire ou circulaire, et te done bien garde en tous tes cauteres que tu n’i lassier mie tant le cautere que tu brules les ners et les grans arteres, et que tu ne faices au malaide plus grant nuisance et contraction.	And if the profession is, and if it is that the pain is outside the groin towards the thigh, then do cauterization with a cauterizing or circular knife, and be very careful in all your cauterizations that you do not leave the cautery for too long so as to burn the nerves and large arteries, and do not cause greater harm and contraction.
Et je meisme ai veus plusors qui ont fait cautere sus la cheville dou piet, et li lasserent tant que li jambe fut toute enflee, et li piez ausi, et fut perciez et corrumpus toz li piez.	And I have also seen many who have done cauterization above the ankle of the foot, and left it for so long that the leg was completely numb, and the feet as well, and all the feet were rotten and corrupted.
Aprés une solution de ventre dont il ot la mort.	After a bout of vomiting that resulted in death.
Et se li dolors est en II parties ensamble, fai cautere en l’une et en l’autre, selonc ceste maniere.	And if the pain is on both sides together, perform cauterization on one and the other, in this manner.
Et li saige dirent en la cautere de la hainche, de coi ci est li maniere, fai I tel fer et soit au chief ausi gros com uns nauvillon de dacte, ou un poc moins, et soit par entrechetres et soit des l’un entrechetres jusc’a l’autre d’espaice la quantiteit d’un nou de poce; et soient li entrechetres aovers de II pars, et soient aussi comme noez, et i ait I mainche de fer bien fait; et c’est li forme:	And the wise say in the cauterization of the waist, because of this manner, use such a sharp knife and as large as a navel-string or slightly less, and cut through and from one to another at a distance equal to the quantity of a finger; and the cuts should be over two parts, and also like a comb, and there should be a good handle of iron; and this is the shape:
Et soit eschaufez tant qu’il soit toz rouges et giete senteles, et puis le mette on sus la boiste de la hainche malaide, et soit tornez sus lou sain costeit; et lou cauterize une fois I cautere reont et lou laisse III jors; et puis fai emplaustre de burre, et laisse la plaie aoverte lonc tens; aprés la cure d’oignement tant qu’il soit sanez.	And let it be heated until it is completely red and has a metallic scent, and then place it on the blister of the painful back, and turn it over to the healthy side; and cauterize once with the cautery when it is hot and leave it for three days; and then apply a poultice of butter, and leave the wound open for a long time; after the care of ointment until it is healed.
Albucasim dit que nos usons poc de cest cautere por la paor de son regart, et se voions poc qui en usent; et toutevoie ceu est des boins cauteres, qui le puet soffrir, et lai ou il s’afiert.	Albucasis says that we use this cautery very little because of its fearsome appearance, and few see those who use it; however, it is a good cauterizer that can withstand it, and where it takes effect.
Li cauteres de medicine ardant si est que tu faices I estrument a entrechetres en coi dessende li marge de la porte, et soit d’arain ou de fer a une paroit longe, et en la hautece ait II nous, et ait entre chaicun la quantiteit de la groissece d’un doi; et soient overt defuer et desus, et se joignent ensamble selonc ceste forme:	The cauteries of burning medicine are such that you make a tool with inserts in the place of the edge of the door, and it is either of brass or iron at one end, and at the top it has II us, and between each quantity of the size of a dove; and they are open below and above, and they join together according to this form:
Aprés met sus la boiste de la hainche au malaide gisant sor suin costeit sain, et apresse ta main mout sus la boiste de la hainche; aprés giete entre les II cercles de l’awe chaude qui soit chaufee au feu I poc, et li laisse une houre dou tens, et soffre li malaides la chalor et l’arsure de li.	After placing the bandage of the hipbone on the patient's back, and quickly placing your hand above the bandage of the hipbone; then pour between the two circles of hot water that has been heated in the fire I poc, and let it stand for an hour, and bear the heat and burning of the wound.
Car il i trueve mordication ausi com de feu; et quant li mordications iert passee, se lieve ta main avec l’estrument et leve la hainche d’awe douce, et laisse ensi III jors, et met sus burre tant que ceu qui est noir de l’eschaudure soit osteit; et lou laisse III jors que porriture en istrait; et ceu serait li derriene aide aprés le cure d’oignemens tant qu’il soit sanez.	Because there is also true mordication as with fire; and when the mordications have passed, let your hand with the instrument and raise the back gently, and leave it for three hours, and put butter on it until the black of the burn is removed; and let it rest for three hours so that it can become more comfortable; and this would be the last aid after the cure of wounds until it is healed.
Et se li dolor s’est estendue jusc’a la cuisse ou jusc’a la jambe, se li fai I estrument que teigne awe selonc ceu que tu as fait en la hainche igaument; et c’est li maniere de l’awe chaude, et je l’ai escripte ou traitier de la rectification de medicine.	And if the pain has spread to the thigh or leg, make the instrument that tingles the back according to what you have done in the waist; and this is the way of the hot wound, and I have written it to treat the correction of medicine.
Pren alcali et chaulz vive, autant de l’une com de l’autre, et les broie ensamble, et les met en I nuef pot.	Take chalk and live charcoal, as much of one as the other, and grind them together, and put them in a new jar.
ou il ait I petit pertuis defuer se que li pointe d’un raisor i puisse entreir; et met desor celui pot I autre pot bien plombeit, et met sus alcali et chalz et awe douce sus, tant qu’il en i ait I doi desus les poudres cant tu l’avras bien preingte a ta main; et le laisse ensi tant qu’il en dessende awe ague et chiece ou pot plombeit, puis pren toute cele awe, et la giete sus chalz et sus alcali si com devant.	And if there is a small hole other than the point of a razor can enter; and put that in the other jar well ground, and put on top of chalk and charcoal and grind gently until you have two above the powders, then you will have it well ground in your hand; and let it stay like that until all the water and juice or what can be ground has dripped off, then take all of this water and pour it on top of chalk and charcoal as before.
Et lors si sera mout ague et est aministree en mou d’ovraiges de medicine et en cauteres d’autres membres Car elle fait auteil oevre com feus, et si a autres medicines dont on cauterize bien la hainche ensi com tesisie et miel anacardi et chalz avec savon, toutes ces choses mellees ensamble.	And if it is very painful and administered in the form of medical work and cauterization of other members because it does such great work as fire, and if it is other medicines that are well cauterized on the back in this way and with anacardium and chalk with soap, all these things mixed together.
Et Galiens nos raconte une cure dont uns hons fut curez de la dolor de la hainche et de la voine sciatique, et lou loe mout, et dit que on n’i fist autre cure, et qu’il en fut sanez a une soule fois quant on ot fait ceste cure, et il se fut baigniez si com il l’enseigne ci aprés.	And Galen tells us of a cure that some people were cured of the pain of the back and sciatica, and it was very effective, and he said that no other cure was made, and that they were well after one time when this cure was made, and he bathed himself as he teaches afterwards.
Et dist en teil maniere que tu preignes dou litargire vert fres et sec, et le broie mout avec I poc de graisse, et met sus la hainche et sus la cuisse et sus la jambe ou la dolor tient, et la lie; et li laisse III houres et par la quantiteit que li malaides ne sente plus l’arsure.	And in this manner, you should apply a fresh, green, and dry willow bark, and grind it thoroughly with a little grease, and place it on the waist and thighs and leg where the pain is, and bind it; and leave it for three hours, and by the quantity that the pains no longer feel the burning.
Et puis le fai entrer ou bain tant que li cors li soit un poc arousez, et lou fai entrer ou lit, et li dolor s’en ira toute et sera sanez.	Then make the patient enter a hot bath until the heart is slightly warm, and then make them lie down, and the pain will go away completely and they will be healed.
Et saiches que nuls ne doit user de cautere de telz medicines, se ceu n’est aprés l’evacuation de cors.	And let it be known that no one should use such medicines with cauterization, unless after the evacuation of blood.
Et Dyascorides dist que quant li voine sciatique est cauterizee de fiens de chievre, si i aide mout; et doit estre fais li cauteres en teil maniere.	And Diocletian says that when the vein sciatic is cauterized with the flesh of a goat, it helps much; and it should be done by cauterizers in this way.
Prenez lainne et la beurez d’oile vielz, et metez sus la fossete qui est entre le pouce dou piez et l’autre qui est apelez foscile.	Take linen and pour old oil into it, and place it on the groove that is between the thumb and the other one called the foreshaft.
Aprés pren fiens de chievre sec, et l’empren a feu tant qu’il soit charbons, et lou met sus la laine, et le laisse tant qu’il soit estains; et refai encor ensi, et ne cesser de faire ensi tant que tu penses par sens qu’il viegne jusc’a la hainche, et que li dolor soit cessee; et cist manieres de cautere est apelez «cautere de chievre».	Then take pieces of dried goat meat and put them in the fire until they are charcoal, and place it on the linen, and let it soak until it is saturated; and do this again and again, and do not stop doing this until you think that it has reached up to the waist, and that the pain has ceased; and this way of cauterizing is called "goat cauterization".
de la dolor dou dos	of great pain to two joints
Quant dolor vient au dos, ou par cheoir ou de percussion ou par trop grant evacuation, ou par semblans de matiere espandue froide, a nule de ces semblances ne vaut cauteres, fuer que a celi qui vient de infusion de froide matiere.	When pain comes to the back, whether from falling or by impact or from too great evacuation, or from similar matters spread out cold, none of these is as effective as cauterizing with hot matter.
Il covient c’aprés ceu que li malaides est voidiez de pilules fetides ou d’autres semblans, que on li faice sus lou dos, lai ou li dolor tient, trois lignes signies d’enche, et en chescune ligne V cauteres ou plus selonc la vertut et la quantiteit que li malaides puet soffrir; et soit fait li cauteres selonc le cautere qui est apelez «poins»; et se tu vues, fai III cauteres ou IIII au cautere clavile moien selonc ceste forme:	It is necessary to apply three lines of charred cloth, soaked in fetid pills or similar matter, on top of the back where the pain is located, and insert five or more cauterizing needles according to the virtue and quantity that the pain can bear; and let the cauterizing needles be made from the cautery called "poins"; and if you see, make three or four needles at the middle cautery called "clavile".
Maintes fois vient ceste maladie as petis enfans, et li signes de l’encomencement si est qu’il ont estroite alainne quant il se lievent, et paor; et tu trueves en la derriene espinee dou dos et en nous l’apparance qui vient sus les autres espinees.	This disease often comes to small children, and the signs of its beginning are that they have a narrow gait when walking, and fear; and you feel it in the last spinous process of the back and in us the appearance that comes above the other spinous processes.
Quant tu vois ceu et tu le vues curer, si le cauterize au cautere de celcle selonc ceste forme.	When you see this and you want to cure it, if you cauterize with the fire cautery according to this form.
Si que li cautere porpreigne chescune partie de l’espinee egaument.	If the fire cautery grasps every part of the spinous process.
Et se tu vues, si cauterize entor l’espinee au cautere poignant II lignes ou III, et soient li poins pres l’uns de l’autre.	And if you see, then cauterize around the spinous process with the fire cautery touching the second or third line, and they are close to each other.
Aprés cure le leu tant qu’il soit sanez selonc ceu que nos avons dit, et warde que tu n’amenistrer cautere en gilbositeit qui soit en spame de nerf.	After treatment, the limb should be kept as we have said, and you must not administer cauterization in a way that causes damage to the nerve.
de la dolor des jointes	The pain of the joints
Quant dolor de jointes sunt de moistors que sont espandues a chaicun membre dou cors, et quant dolor vient em piez, que li mire apelent «podagre» proprement, et quant elle est de froide cause et cures de medicines ne la puent curer, si est curez par cauteres en teil maniere: fai li mout de cauteres entor la jointure dou piet, et soit li cauteres olivaire selonc ceste forme:	When the pain of the joints is due to moisture that has spread to each limb of the body, and when the pain comes suddenly, which is properly called "gout", and when it is caused by cold and is not cured by medicines, then it must be treated with cauterization in this way: apply a lot of cauterizing agent around the joint, and the cauterizing agent should be olive oil in this form:
Et s’il i a besoigne que tu poignes sus la faice dou piet, se li fai cautere a tot le cautere c’on claime «point».	And if there is a time when you must hold the face down, then perform the entire cauterization as claimed by the term "point".
Et se les dolors viegnent jusc’a genous et as autres jointures, et ceu avient maintes fois, se li fai cautere sus chaicun genoil III cauteres ou IIII de chescunne partie, a tout le cautere olivaire; et se tu as mestier de plus, si en fai plus, mais n’i tenir mie ta main fuers que tant que li espés dou keur soit ars.	And if the pain comes from the jaw and other joints, and it happens often, then perform cauterization with three or four cauteries on each part of the lower jaw; and if you have more skill, do more, but do not hold your hand further than the tip of the healer's knife.
Et se les dolors dessendent jusc’a genoil et au dos, se li aministre le cautere que nos avons dit en son chapistre.	And if the pain descends to the jaw and the back, then administer the cauterization that we have mentioned in its chapter.
Et se les dolors sunt as mains, si fai poins entor le foscile II lignes; et s’il remaint point de dolor as dois, si fai poins sus chescune jointe et sus lou poil de la main; et se les dolors vienent jusc’as coutes ou jusc’as espaules, si cauterize chescune partie, et fai boin governement au malaide et penre medicines.	If the pains are on the hands, do pinches around the finger II lines; and if they remain not painful, do pinches on each joint and on the hair of the hand; and if the pains come just after the wrist or shoulder, cauterize each part, and give good management to the patient and appropriate medicines.
Car se tu li fais boin governement et tu purges fleume, si sera saneis a l’aide de Deu.	For if you give good management and purge the humor, it will be healed with the help of God.
de la routure dou syfac	of the tearing of the skin
Quant routure vient en angres, et li bouelz dessendent as coions et c’est novelement, si covient que quant tu lou vues curer, qu’il ne menjuce mie celui jor; et qu’il use choses qui laichent lou ventre, si que li fiens dessende de son ventre; aprés le fai seoir sus son dos entre tes mains, et li comande qu’il teigne son alaine tant que li boueil soient repairiet, et les ramoinne a tes dois, et seigne d’enche desoz la routure sus l’os dou poignil, et a tout un signe que soit semblans a la moitiet d’un cercle a desus dou cors; puis eschaufe le cautere de coi ci est li forme:	When the tearing comes in anger, and the pus descends to the ankles and this is not new, if you see that it needs to be healed, that it does not move much that day; and that you use things that make the belly expand, so that the wounds descend from his belly; afterwards, make him sit on his back between your hands, and command him to stretch his arm as long as the pus is repaired, and bring them to your own, and seize off the wound over the bone of the little finger, and all a sign that is similar to half a circle above the body; then heat the cautery with this form:
tant qu’il soit blans et qu’il giete senteles.	so long as it is white and sweats scents.
Puis ramoine les bouels a lor leu; et li ministres teigne sa main sus qu’il ne retornent arrier; et oevre bien les cuisses au malaide, et met desoz lui I cussin et I serjant sus les cuisses, et I autre sus lou pis qui li teigne les mains; puis met le cautere sus lou signe a tout ta main, et lou tien droit et lou tien tant que tu ateignes l’os, et se tu ne l’ateins la premiere fois, si le rencomence encor une autre tant que tu viegnes jusc’a l’os; et te warde subtilment que li boueil ne saille quant tu fais lou cautere; que tu ne le brulasses; et que par ceu li malaides ne muere, ou autre malz.	Then remove the dirt from the joint; and the assistant stains his hand above it so that it does not return backwards; and work well the thighs at the injury, and put some ointment and some salve on them, and the other on the worst one that stains his hands; then put the cautery on the sign all over your hand, and hold it straight and hold it until you reach the bone, and if you do not reach it the first time, start again with another until you come near to the bone; and be careful that the dirt does not come out while you are doing the cautery; that you do not burn it; and that by this the pain does not kill him, or any other harm.
Et saiches que quant tu ne viens jusc’a l’os au cautere, tes ovraiges ne vaut rien.	And when you do not see the bone at the fire cauterization, your works are worthless.
Et covient que li cauteres des enfans soit subtilz selonc la mesure d’ous, et des grans gens aussi grans selonc lor mesure; aprés III jors cure lou leu dou cautere de burre tant que li eschaudure soit ostee; aprés le cure d’autres oignemens tant qu’il soit sanez, et gise li malaides XL jors sus son dos tant que li plaie soit bien soudee; et covient que ses norrissemens soit lassatis longement, si que li boueil ne saillent quant il se preigdra d’aler en chambres.	And it is necessary that the cauterizer of children be subtle according to the measure of their age, and large people accordingly; after three days care for the wound of the fire cauterization until the scar is healed; then care for other injuries as long as they are healthy, and grind the hairs on their back forty days after the wound is well healed; and it is necessary that their stools be loose for a long time, so that the bile does not rise when they go to the chamber.
Et aprés XL jors, quant il se voudra lever, se li amenistre une faixe bien faite, et la porse XL autres jors; et ait boin repos, qu’il se travaille poc et se warde de trop grant repletion de boivre et de mengier, et de trop haut braire; et quant il fait cest enseignement si est sanez entierement.	And after forty days, when he wishes to rise, give him a fine bandage and leave it for forty more days; let him have good rest, working little and avoiding too much drinking and eating, and too much heat; and when he follows this instruction, he is entirely healed.
Et je dirai ci aprés la cure de taillier en son chapistre.	And I will say what to do after the treatment of cutting into his chapter.
de la routure dou ventre	of the rupture of the belly
Quant routures vienent en autres ventres et sont connisans, et tu vues qu’elles ne croissent plus, se li fai I cautere dou cautere reont selonc sa quantiteit, et soit ars li tiers dou keur; aprés le cure selonc ceu que nos avons dit; et aucun des anciens ont dit c’on le doit cauterizer au cautere a III angles selonc ceste forme:	When ruptures come in other bellies and are known, and you see that they do not grow anymore, then apply the fire cautery according to its quantity, and let one-third of the healing be done; after the treatment, according to what we have said; and none of the ancients have said that it should be cauterized with the cautery at three angles according to this form:
mais signe premier le leu d’enche et fai une ligne per la largesce desus la routure, et une autre defuers, et main ta main emmi a tout le cautere clavile.	but the first sign is the swelling of the limb and make a line across the width above the tear, and another below, and hold your hand on all the cauterizing iron.
Mais li premiers cauteres est plus legiers et muedres.	But the first cauteries are lighter and more painful.
de dolor anciene en aucun membre	of ancient pain in any limb
Quant dolor vient en aucun membre, ou de cheoir ou de ferir, et cele dolor tient lonc tens, et li cure de medicine n’i vaut, adonc covient qu’il soit cauterizeis au cautere qui est apelez «poins», et soit li cauteres selonc la longesce dou membre et la petitece et sa foibleteit et sa vertut et sa location de torcions et de sa dolor.	When pain comes to any limb, or to fall or to be injured, and this pain lasts long, and the medical cure does not help, then it is necessary to cauterize with the cauterizing iron called «poins», and the cauteries should follow the length of the limb and its smallness and its weakness and its strength and its location of twists and its pain.
s’il est sanez dou premier cautere, c’est bien; se ceu nom, recomence I autre cautere sus celui, car teilz costume est qu’il se doit muer au membre que li est prochiens, por coi il covient que tu faices les cauteres tant que li malaides soit saneis.	If the first cauterization is done well, it is good; if not, start another cauterization on top of the first one, for it is often customary that it must die to the member that is closest, so you should do the cauterizations until the wounds are healed.
de meselerie	of medical instruments
Li meseil sont aidiet aucune fois par cautere par grant aide, et meismement li maladie que vient de la putrefaction de fleume et de melancolie.	Medical instruments are often not helped by cauterization due to great harm, and at the same time, the disease that comes from the putrefaction of fluids and melancholy.
Cant tu la vues cauterizer, pren warde se li maladie est au comencement, et s’ele est curee selonc ceu que nos avons dit en la division, et ne dessent ne ne demoure, et tu doutes que li corruption ne porpreigne tout le malaide, adonques li fai V cauteres sus lou chief: I emmi le chief a nouf, et l’autre vers lou front a la fin des chevous; et II sus les II cornes, et I derrierre sus le haiterel; et i laise tant ta main que li cauteres viegne jusc’a l’os, et tant que les escorces en issent fors si que les vapors des grosses humors s’en puissent issir; et le cauterize sus la mice selonc ce qu’il est devant.	If you see the wound cauterized, take care if the disease is at the beginning, and if it has been cured according to what we have said in the division, and does not spread or remain, and you doubt that corruption will not spread throughout the wound, then do three cauterizations: I on the front of the head, and the other towards the forehead at the end of the eyebrows; II over the two corners, and I behind the temple; and leave as much space as the cauterization comes to the bone, and as long as the scabs come out so that the vapors of large humors can escape; and cauterize the small one according to what is in front.
Et se li meselerie est partout esparse; et elle pert manifestement, si covient que tu lou cauterizes de ces cauteres que nos avons dit ou chief, et I cautere en som lou neis, et II cauteres sus l’espinee dou col, et VI cauteres sus l’espinee dou dos, et I grant sus la crupie et I autre delez, et II sus les II espaules; et II sus les coutes, et II sus les tendrons dou pis, et I sus chascune jointe des mains et des piez, et sus les fosses des mains; et te warde des ners que sunt sus lou derrien calcant, que tu ne les bruler; et aucune fois fait om cautere sus l’os dou poignil, et I autre sus l’os de l’estomac, et I autre sus lou foie.	If the injury is scattered throughout; and it is clearly present, then you must cauterize with these cauteries that we have mentioned or chief, and the cautery in the middle of the nose, and two cauteries above the spine of the neck, and six cauteries above the spine of the back, and one great one above the hindquarters and one other below, and two above the shoulders, and two above the elbows, and two above the knees, and one above each joint of the hands and feet, and above the wounds of the hands; and be careful of the nerves that are above the calcaneus, that you do not burn them; and never make a cauterization above the bone of the wrist, and one above the bone of the stomach, and one above the liver.
Et saiches que quant plus i fais de cautere, plus li fais d’aide, et mues li profite; et saiches que li malaides ne sent point de dolor au cautere si com li sain le sentent, por ce que li cors est ja toz corrumpus.	And so it is that the more you perform cauterization, the less you need to provide assistance, and it benefits him; and so it is that the pains are not felt as much at cauterization as they are by the healthy person, because the body is already corrupted.
Et covient ke li cautere soient grant et petit selonc les membres et les jointures, selonc ceu que vos lou troverez en manieres des fers.	It is necessary that the cauterization be large and small according to the members and the joints, as you will find in the methods of irons.
Aprés cure lou leu de farine de veces avec miel et autres cures tant qu’il soit saneis.	After curing the wound with flour several times with honey and other treatments until it is healed.
Quant enfleure vient en aucun membre et est curee par medicines et oiles et emplastres, et il n’est mie sanez, adonques li fai cauteres sus le membre selonc la grandour et la petitece dou membre; et soit li cauteres un poc entrans en l’espés dou keur; puis le cure d’oignemens tant qu’il soit sanez.	When inflammation comes to any member and is treated with medicines, oils, and plasters, and it is not healed, then perform cauterization on the member according to its size and smallness; and let the cauterization go a little into the skin; then treat the wounds until it is healed.
Et aucune fois fait on cautere et a la main et au piet et au dos, a l’issue dou nerf que muet le membre, et ensi si est ostee li enfleure; et toutevoie ne s’en entremette nuls s’il n’est conoissans des membres et des issues des ners movans lou cors.	And never does one cauterize with the hand and at the elbow and at the back, at the end of the nerve that moves the limb, and thus it is osteopathic if it inflames; and it does not interfere with anything if one does not know the members and their issues from the nerves moving the body.
de albaras	For the barbarians
Quant li maladie qui est apelee «albaras» est enveillie, et li engien de medicine n’i valent rien, adonques le cauterize d’un cautere un poc parfont, selonc la quantiteit de l’espés dou keur, tant que li blenchour soit ostee, et soit muee sa color; puis le cure de farine de veces et de lentilles avec oile roset et foilles de plantain, et sanc de colon et sanc d’alondre, de chescun une partie; et soit mellez tout ensamble, et soit liiez d’un drapel, et soit aers au leu tant qu’il soit sanez.	When the disease called "barbarian" is awakened, and medical science has no effect on it, then cauterize with a cautery a little in advance, according to the quantity of the herb, until the swelling is hardened, and its color is changed; then treat with flour and lentils with rose oil and plantain leaves, and of each one part; and mix everything together, and apply as a poultice on the affected area, and bandage with a cloth, and keep it to the limb until it is healed.
li cure de chancre par cautere	the treatment of chancres by cauterization
Quant chancre vient au comencement, et tu lou vues arrester, si le cauterize au cautere qui semble I cercle, tout entor au tour dou chancre.	When a chancres appears at the beginning, and you see it stop spreading, then cauterize it with a cautery that seems like a circle, all around the circumference of the chancres.
Et toutevoie li saige dirent que on faice cautere ausi au mileu dou chancre; et toutevoie ceu ne me semble mie boin, car je redous que il ne soit ulcerez et corrumpus, et je l’ai ja veut avenir aucune fois; et plus droituriere chose est qu’il soit cauteriés entor, au cautere qui est apelez «circule», si com nos avons dit en mout de cauteres.	And everyone says that one should also make a cautery in the middle of the chancres; and I do not think this is good, because I believe it should not be ulcerated and corrupted, and I have never seen it happen; and the better thing is that it be cauterized around, with the cautery that is called «circle», as we have said in many cauterizations.
de l’enfleure qui ne puet meurer	of the swelling that cannot die
Quant aucuns ait une maladie qui est apelee «adubelati», et elle tarde de meurer ou por la superfluiteit qu’ele fait ou por l’eaige dou malaide quant il est decrepites (c’est a dire trop vielz) et il a poc de sanc, ou por lou tens; et tu la vues haster de meurer: adonques le cauterize entor de mout de petis cauteres en poignant; aprés le laisse ensi.	When anyone has a disease called "adubelati", and it lingers on the brink of death due to the excess it causes or because of the age-related weakness when they are too old, and they have little blood, or due to tension; then you see it hastening towards death: therefore cauterize around with many small cauteries pricking; afterwards leave it thus.
Car elle se hastera de meureir.	For it will hasten to die.
Et se tu la vues percier a tout le cautere, si chaufe le cautere de coi ci est li forme:	And if you see it pierced by the entire cauterization, then warm up the cauterization from where this is the form:
Et met ta main en mileu de cele maladie qui est apellee «adubelati» tant que li cauteres ait perciet lou keur, et soit telz li cauteres que li malaides lou sente defuers en teil maniere que li cours de la porriture soit alegis.	And place your hand in the middle of this disease called "adubelati" until the cauteries have pierced the skin, and be such cauteries that the pain felt before is in a similar manner to the course of the porridge is alleviated.
Aprés le cure tant qu’il soit sanez parfaitement.	After the treatment until he is completely healed.
li cure dou feu par fer	The treatment of fire by iron
Une autre maniere de maladie i a qui est apelee «corrodens», et n’est autre chose que une mengeson de membre, car ele menjut les membres ausi com li feus les leignes seches.	Another way of disease is called "corrodens", and it is nothing other than a piece of member, for it twists the members as if the dry reeds would.
Se tu vois ceste maladie en leu qui puisse soffrir cautere ensamble feu, adonques eschaufe les cauteres clavile mout petit et grant, selonc ceu qu’il covient au leu ou li maladie est; aprés le cauterize de toutes pars tant que tu erraiche toute la corruption, et nen remaigne rien de li, que tout ceu qui est corrumpus ne soit osteit.	If you see this disease in the leg that can suffer cauteries together with fire, then heat the cauteries with a small and great knife, according to what is needed for the leg or the disease; after cauterizing all parts until you reach all the corruption, and nothing remains of it, so that all that is corrupted is removed.
Et puis le laisse III jors, et met sus les leus cauterizez soffre broiet avec oile tant que les eschaudures dou feu soient ostees, et toute li corruption.	And then leave it for three days, and apply a poultice with oil over the wounds until the burnt flesh is removed and all the corruption.
Aprés lou cure d’oignemens engendrans char.	After the treatment of boils, they generate carbuncles.
Et se tu vois aprés III jors que chars saine ne naisse, c’est boin; et se ceu non, si rencomence le cautere sus ceu qui est demoreit des leus corrumpus.	And if you see after three days that healthy char does not arise, it is good; and if not, then start the fire cautery again on the remaining corrupted parts.
Et ceste mengeson est aucune fois esteit curee de medicine ague en leu de cautere de feu; mais toutevoie cautere de feu est de plus grant aide, et j’ai ja dit la cure de la medicine ague en la division: pren la quant tu en as mestier.	And this method has never been treated with medicine in place of the fire cautery; but the fire cautery is of greater help, and I have already told the treatment of the medicine ague in the division: take it when you have business.
des porrelz qui vienent as piez	of the peas that come to the feet
Mout de fois avient que as piez par defuers naist une maladie qui est apelee «clos» selonc nostre entencion, et est une grosse chose fautree qui blece lou piet.	Many times it comes to the feet by defect, and a disease arises which is called "clubfoot" according to our understanding, and it is a great disfigurement that makes the foot ugly.
Et li cauteres de ceste maladie si est selonc II manieres.	And the cauteries of this disease are according to two methods.
C’est a savoir cautere de feu, et cautere d’aigue chaude.	That is to say, fire cauterization, and water cauterization with hot iron.
Cautere de feu si est que tu eschaufe I cautere cheveit ausi com est une penne de vouteul, et soit fait de boin fer a la mesure qu’il puisse porpenre le clou de toutes pars, et qu’il i ait subtilz marges; aprés le met tout chaut sus lou clou, et torne ta main tot entor le clou tant qu’il viegne au font dou clou; et lou laisse ensi III jors tant qu’il encomence giter porriture; puis li fai un emplaustre de malves savaiges broiies avec seil, et laisse l’emplaustre sus toute la nuit, et li clous cherra et sera desracinez de ses racines.	Fire cauterization is done by heating the cautery as if it were a pen quill, and it should be made of good iron at the measure that it can penetrate the nail from all parts, and that it has thin margins; after placing it all hot on top of the nail, turn your hand entirely around the nail until it comes to the end of the nail; and leave it thus for three days until it begins to rot; then make an ointment of wild sage leaves boiled with oil, and leave the ointment on all night, and the nail will fall off and be removed from its roots.
Puis cure le leu d’oignement enjanrant char tant qu’il soit sanez.	Then cure the joint with poultice applying hot char until it is healed.
Et s’il sont convertit par defuers lou cors, et maintes fois avient et en mains et em piez, si covient que tu i amenistres cautere d’aigue chaude; et est en teil maniere: pren une cainne d’arain ou de fer, ou une penne de vouteul, et met sus lou clou et l’althelul, c’est asavoir porrelz verrues; et met la cainne sus si qu’ele porpreigne tout entor, puis i met un poc d’awe chaude, et retien bien ta main, et presse ta main en tornant si que li marge de la cainne viegne a la racine dou clou, et puisse trover l’aigue chaude voie parfonde jusc’a la racine; et soffre li malaides un poc la mordication de l’aigue chaude une houre; puis le laisse ensi, et il se derracinera tous a tout ses racines.	And if they are converted by previous wounds, and often in the hands and feet, it is necessary that you reapply cauterization with very hot iron; and it is in this way: take a needle of iron or steel, or a quill pen, and place it on the nail and the cuticle, that is to say, the veruca; then put a drop of very hot water, and hold your hand firmly, and press your hand so that the edge of the needle comes to the root of the nail, and find the very hot water path deeply up to the root; and let the pain of the very hot water for an hour; then leave it like this, and it will all fall out at all its roots.
Ensi fai un aprés autre, tant que tu esraiches toz ces qui sont au cors, puis les cure des oignemens qui engenrent char.	After doing another one like this, remove all those who are in the chest, then treat the boils that cause char.
li cure dou trembler	the cure for trembling
Quant aucuns tremble de froidor de ners, ou de fievre quartaine ou d’autre, si covient que tu li faices IIII cauteres ou IV sus l’espinee dou dos, I cautere entre chescune espinee; et I cautere ou pez, et I sus l’estomac au cautere olivaire; si laissera lou trembler, et se hastera li santez de la maladie froide.	When anyone trembles from cold or from a fourth-day fever or other, it is necessary to make four cauteries or four on the spine of the back; one cautery between each spine; and one cautery above the stomach at the olive cautery; it will leave the trembling, and hasten the recovery from the illness.
des pustules puans	of pus-filled boils
Aucune fois apperent par defuers le cors bathes, ou pustules puans, que vienent de grosses matieres corrumpues.	No times have appeared previously when the chest was bathed with pus and pustules that come from large corrupt matter.
si covient au premier quant eles apperent que on faice cautere sus chescun chief de la pustule: un cautere subtil de fust de mirte, de coi li pointe soit emprise au feu, ou de racine de aristologe longe, ou au cautere lenticulaire.	If it is necessary to perform a cauterization on each pustule when they appear: a subtle fire-tipped wand of myrtle, from which the point is grasped in the fire, or of long aristoloch root, or with a lenticular cauterizer.
Et aucune fois les cauterize on au comencement quant il aperent, selonc ceste maniere, et il ne puent croistre des enqui en avant, mais est desrompue li superfluitez dont il vienent, et sont sanez; mais il covient que ceu soit fait aprés l’evacuation de sanc.	And never cauterize at the beginning when they appear, according to this method, and it cannot grow further, but is broken down by the excess from which they come, and are healed; but it is necessary that this be done after the evacuation of blood.
quant li artere est copee	when the artery is cut
Maintes fois avient grans decorremens de sanc de l’artere qui est copee a la plaie que vient au pardefuers, ou a l’incision de l’aposteme, ou au cautere dou membre, et as semblans choses; et est mout grief chose d’estenchier.	often there is great bleeding from the artery that is cut at the wound which comes to the periphery, or at the incision of the abscess, or at the cauterization of the member, and similar things; and it is a very difficult thing to stop.
Et toutevoie quant ceu avient a aucun, si te haste de mettre ton doi indice sus la plaie de la voinne, et l’estrain mout tant que li sans soit apaisiez desoz ton doi, et que goute n’en isse plus; puis met au feu les cauteres olivaire plusors petis et grans tant qu’il soient tuit rouge; puis empren I, ou grant ou petit selonc la plaie et lou leu en coi li artere est route, et met le cautere sus cele voine ou tu tiens ton doi, et tien le cautere tant sus que li sans soit restainchiez.	And whenever this happens to anyone, you must quickly place your finger on the wound of the vein, and press it very tightly until the bleeding is stopped, and no more blood comes out; then put the cauterizing irons on fire several times large and small as long as they are all red; then apply I, or a great or small one according to the wound and the limb in which the artery is located, and place the cauterizing iron on that vein where you hold your finger, and keep the cauterizing iron there until the bleeding is stopped.
Et s’il saut fuers quant tu lieves ton doi desus la voinne, et li cauteres estint, si pren hastivement I autre des cauteres qui sont au feu.	And if you have to lift your elbow quickly when lifting the vein, and the cautery is extinguished, then take the other cautery that is at the fire.
Et ne cesser de faire ceu l’un aprés l’autre tant que li sans soit estenchiez; et warde que tu n’ardes lou nerf qui est delez, et que autre malice ne viegne sus lou malaide; et saiches que quant sans decourt de l’artere, c’on ne lou puet mie bien restenchier meismement quant li artere est grans, se ceu n’est par une des IIII manieres que nos avons dit: ou par cautere, ou par extraction quant ele n’est mie traite, ou par fort liement de fil, ou par medicines mises sus qui ont pooir de restenchier sanc; et soit liee et estrainte avennament.	And do not stop doing this one after the other until the blood is extinguished; and be careful not to burn the nerve that is next to it, and that no other harm comes over the wound; and remember that when the artery is not cut off, it cannot be extinguished directly when the artery is large, unless by one of the four methods that we have said: or by cautery, or by extraction when it is not yet treated, or by a strong thread, or by medicines placed over which have power to extinguish blood; and let it be tied and held firmly.
Qui i amenistrera restenchement de liier estroitement de drapelz ou de metre choses ardans sus, ou autres semblans choses, se n’i profite se poc non.	Whoever administers tight binding with cloths or other things burning above, or similar things, does not benefit if not done carefully.
Et se ce avient a aucun et il n’ait mie mire ne medicine present, si doit mettre son doi indice sus la plaie de la voinne si com nos avons dit, et bien estrendre tant qu’il soit restenchiez desus la plaie et desus la voinne; et ne remuer lou doit, mais lou moille d’awe froide sovent que soit mout froide tant que li sans soit congelez et engrossiez et restenchiez; et faice des enqui en avant ceu dont il a mestier de cauteres et de medicines.	And if this happens to anyone and they have no other remedy or medicine present, they should place their finger index on the wound of the vein as we have said, and tightly bind it until it is cauterized above the wound and above the vein; and they should not move it, but keep it cold with a cool cloth often until it is frozen and swollen and cauterized; and make inquiries about what they need for cauterization and medicines.
Ci encomence li secons livre des cures de taille	Here begins the second book of remedies for wounds
Nos vos avons dit ou premier chapistre toute maladie en coi il covient cautere de feu, ou de medicine ardans, et les oquisons et les causes et les estrumens et les formes des cauteres; et ai mis celui chapistre des lou chief jusc’a piez, et je irai en cest chapistre par celi meisme voie por ceu c’on trueve plus legierement ceu c’on voura.	We have told you in the first chapter all diseases for which it is necessary to cauterize with fire, or with burning medicine, and the questions and causes and instruments and forms of cauteries; and I will put this chapter about the shoulder joint down to the feet, and I will go to this chapter by this same way because one can find more easily what one wants.
Et ainsois que je encomence ceu, il covient, chier fil, que vos aprenez que en cest chapistre a plus de peril et de paor que ou premier des cauteres, et por ceu il covient plus grant cautele.	And therefore when I begin this chapter, it is necessary, dear child, that you learn that in this chapter there is more danger and fear than in the first of the cauteries, and for this reason it is necessary to take greater precaution.
Car en l’ovraige de cest chapistre avient maintes fois evacuation de sanc a l’ovrir la voinne, et a l’incision sus aposteme, et as cures des plaies, et a l’estraction des saiettes, et a l’incision sus la piere, et les semblans choses; ou il a doutance et paor, et en vient li mors a plusors.	For in the work of this chapter, there has often been the evacuation of blood when opening a vein, and incising an abscess, and in the treatment of wounds, and in the extraction of arrows, and in cutting into stones, and similar things; where there is doubt and fear, and many die.
Et je vos amoneste que vos n’entreprenez folie.	And I warn you that you should not undertake foolishness.
Car mout de manieres de gens vienent en cures.	For many methods of people come for cure.
si vienent de telz qui s’aïrent si avec lor maladie qu’il muerent legierement por la forsenerie qu’il trueve de sa maladie, et de la grandour de son malice; et de ces doit on avoir paor.	If they come from such people who are so with their illness that they die immediately because of the harm they find in their disease, and the greatness of its evil; and of these one must have fear.
Et de ces i a qui te done son sens, et dit: «atendez, je sui garis»; et li maladie est despitouse.	And of these, there are those who give you their sense, and say: "Wait, I am sick"; and the disease is spiteful.
Il ne covient mie que vos vos consentez a ces qui vienent a vos qui ont ceste maniere, mais mettez plus grant cusanson en vostre honor qu’en vostre covoitise, et n’ovrez mie folement mais saigement de ceu dont vos estes certain, et dont vos poez avoir pris et los; et usez de pronostication et de indication en cures de vos malaides a coi salus soit convertie; et ceu vos aidera a aquester bone renommee, et gloire, et memoire de loenge.	It is not enough that you grant consent to those who come to you who have this manner, but put greater caution in your honor than in your need, and do not open rashly but wisely of that of which you are certain, and which you have taken and lost; and use prognosis and indication in the treatment of your illnesses so that health may be converted; and this will help you to acquire good reputation, glory, and memory for a long time.
Tres chier fil, Nostres Sires vos doint boin entendement et droiture, et se vos vuelle espireir de la sainte inspiration de sa main, amen.	Very dear son, Our Lords grant you good understanding and rightness, and if you wish to breathe from the holy inspiration of His hand, amen.
Or je vos ai ordeneit cest chapistre en devisant par chapistres, selonc ceu qu’il est devant ou chapistre des cauteres, que je vos ai deviseit des le chief jusc’a piez, por ceu que vos trovez plus legierement ceu dont vos avrez mestier.	Or I have ordered you this chapter by dividing it into sections, according to what is before or after the chapter on cauteries, that I have divided from the beginning to the end, because you will find it more easily what you will have to do.
dou chief plein d’aigue	The beginning full of sharp
Saiches que ceste maladie vient mout de fois as enfans a l’enfanter, et quant li baille estraint trop fort le chief de l’enfant; et aucune fois vient ceu de cause reponue que on ne seit.	This disease often comes to children at birth, and when the child's head is held too tightly; and sometimes it comes from a cause that is not understood why.
Et je ne vis onques ceste maladie fuers qu’en enfans, et a toz ces que j’ai veus se hastait li mors; et por ceu me semble qu’il me vaut mues lassier l’ovraige en teilz cures.	I have never seen this disease except in children, and all those I have seen died; and since it seems to me that it is better to learn about these treatments in advance.
Et je vis I enfant de coi li chiés estoit plains d’aigue, et li chief engroissoit chescun jor tant qu’il ne lou pooit sostenir; et crut tant li moistor qu’il fut mors, et ceste moistor si est assemblee desoz l’os sus lou syphac, entre lou keur et l’os; et li ovraiges si est telz se li moistor est entre lou keur et l’os, et li apostemes est petis, que tu fendes emmi lou chief une fendure large; et soit ausi longe com II nous, tant que li mostor corre; et vez ci la forme dou spatumile:	I saw a child who was suffering from severe pain in the shoulder, and the head was swelling each day until it could not be supported; and it was so much moisture that it died, and this moisture is assembled outside the bone above the shoulder blade, between the skin and the bone; and the treatments are such that if the moisture is between the skin and the bone, and the abscesses are small, you should make a large incision in the head; and it should be as long as two fingers, so that the moisture flows out; and then remove the form of the sponge.
Se li moistor est plus creue, et li aposteme soit plus grans, si fai II fendures en maniere d’une croix, selonc ceste forme:	If the moisture is more abundant, and the abscess is larger, then make two incisions in the form of a cross, according to this shape:
Et se li moistor est desoz l’os, et li signes que tu vois les commissures dou chief overtes de chescune partie, et li aigue saut fuer quant tu la presses de ta main au dedens, et ceu ne t’est mie reponut: si covient que tu fendes enmi lou chief III fendures selonc ceste maniere:	And if the moisture is outside the bone, and the signs that you see the commissures of the joint are open on each side, and the sharp pain is great when you press it with your hand inside, and it does not respond: then you must make three incisions in the joint according to this manner:
Et aprés l’incision estrai la moistor toute fuers.	And after the incision, drain all the moisture out.
Aprés estraint les fendures de drapelz et de poudres, et i met vin et oile, et laisse ensi jusc’a cinquieme jor; puis le deslie, et cure la plaie par tentes et par oignemens, et laisse estraindre le chief egaument, et done mengier au malaide viande seche de poc de moistor tant que li membre soit confortez et sanez.	After the incisions are dressed with bandages and powders, and put wine and oil on it, and leave it in this way until the fifth day; then remove it, and cure the wound with tents and counter-irritants, and keep the joint immobile, and gradually introduce dry food without moisture until the limb is comfortable and healthy.
Et une autre maniere d’incision est que tu regardes ou apert li grandor de l’aposteme, et li assemblé de l’aigue; car aucune fois est elle devant; aucune fois derrier; aucune fois en destre; et aucune fois en senestre.	And another way of incision is that you look at the size of the abscess and the position of the sharp; for it is never before, never behind, never on the right, and never on the left.
Taille donques lai ou li aposteme apert, et l’emplissement de l’aigue, et lou fent selonc ce que tu en as le pooir; et warde que tu ne coper l’artere; et veigne flun de sanc, si que li malaides muere dou decorrement de sanc et de l’evacuation de moistor.	Therefore cut out the size of the abscess and fill it with sharp, and do so according to what you have the power; and be careful not to cover the artery; and if there is blood flow, so that the pain dies down due to the discharge of blood and the evacuation of moisture.
de reume	of return
Quant il avient a aucun une maladie qui est apelee «catarre» as eulz ou au pis, et li maladie est anciainne, et li cure de medicine ne profite mie, adonques li derraine cure si est li cauteres avec ceu c’on li copera les II arteres.	When it comes to any disease that is called "cataract" on those or in the foot, and the disease is ancient, and the medical treatment does not help much, then the treatment is to cauterize with what they cover the two arteries.
Il covient donques, cant tu les vues coper, que li malaides faice rere son chief; aprés li frotte lou leu d’un drapel aspre tant que les arteres aperent, puis estraingne li malaides son col a tout I drapel; puis regarde ou li voine bait, et li leus de l’une et de l’autre sont aprés les oreilles, et poc sont reponues; puis signe les leus d’enche, puis cope l’une et l’autre d’un spatumile agut de II pars, tant que li taille veigne jusc’a l’os, et ceu soit par lou large dou chief.	It is therefore necessary, while you view the wounds, that the hairs make their way back to their heads; after that, rub the limb with a rough cloth until the arteries appear, then hold the hairs against the cloth in all directions; then look where the blood is coming from, and the veins on both sides are behind the ears, and they are not yet closed; then sign the veins to close, then cover both with a sponge of two parts agar, until the wound comes close to the bone, and it should be through the width of the head.
Et se tu vues, boute le spatumile desoz l’artere et la cope au desus, en taillant ausi com II dois au traver.	And if you see, pour out the sponge outside the artery and cover it above, cutting in the same way as it should be through the middle.
Et quant li voinne est copee, si saut li sans en haut continuelment fuers.	And when the vein is cut, let it bleed continuously until it stops on its own.
Et se li artere n’apert au sentir, si covient que tu mesures la quantiteit de l’espaice de III dois, puis seigne d’enche et fent jusc’a l’os; et ceu qu’il covient dou sanc mettre fuers si est VI c/, et par aventure un poc plus ou moins, selonc ce que li malaides puet soffrir, et la repletion de l’artere; puis regarde la plaie: s’il remaint sus l’os point dou syphac, si le cope que apostemes chaus n’i veigne, puis estrain la plaie et lie, et la cure d’oignement tant qu’ele soit sanee.	And if the artery does not open on its own, it is necessary to measure the amount of space between three fingers, then insert and press against the bone; and if six centimeters of blood needs to be removed, and perhaps a little more or less depending on how much the wound can bear, and the replacement of the artery; then look at the wound: if it remains above the bone pointed downwards, and the suture that was applied does not bleed, then cover the wound and bind it, and treat the wound with ointment until it is healed.
de emigrainne	for the head of the shoulder
Quant emigrainne anciaine vient, et catarre agut, por les moistors des larmes et les chalors en temples et sode anciene forsenee et semblans choses, et il est medicinez par manieres de cures de medicine et tout ceu ne li profite mie, si estraions les arteres des temples et lou cauterizons, si com nos avons conteit.	when the ancient head of the shoulder comes, and it is stuck due to the moisture of tears and chills in the temples and old age and similar things, and it is treated by means of medical cures and nothing helps him, then we should cauterize the arteries of the temples and burn, as we have said.
Et li maniere de l’estraction d’elles si est que li malaides faice rere les poilz de ses temples, et entende a l’artere qui apert en la temple, car elle apert bien par son batement, et est poc reponue fuers que en aucuns homes qui sont trop froit; et s’elle est reponue, si estraigne son col li malaides d’aucuns drapelz, puis frote le leu d’aucun aspre drap, et arose le leu d’aigue chaude tant que li artere apere manifestement; puis pren le spatumile de coi ci est li forme:	And the method of extracting them is that the hairs of his temples are made to face backwards, and he understands the artery that opens in the temple, because it opens well by its beating, and it is not replaced until in any man who is too cold; and if it is replaced, then strain the skin with some cloths, then rub the skin with some rough cloth, and raise the skin with hot water until the artery opens clearly; then take the spatula of which this form is made:
puis escorche le cuir legierement tant que tu veignes a l’artere, puis la trai en haut as pinceures, et la depart bien des toiles que sont desoz li de chescune partie; et se li artere est subtilz, si la torne a la pointe de l’uncine, puis la cope de celle partie selonc la quantiteit des II chiés.	Then gently scrape the skin until you reach the artery, then cut it at the top with pincers, and remove all the threads that are attached to each part; if the artery is thin, turn it to the tip of the needle, then cover that part according to the amount of the two joints.
Car s’elle n’est copee, si ne saut mie li sans dou tout en tout.	But if it is not covered, it will not jump all at once.
Et trai dou sanc des VI c/, jusc’a III; et se li artere est grans, si covient que tu la lies en II leus d’un fil double fort de soie, que porriture n’i veigne devant le soudement de la plaie, et veigne decorremens de sanc; puis cope la superfluiteit qui est entre les II liiens en celle houre meisme, et puis, se tu vues, si lou cauterize dou cautere cutellaire jusc’a l’os tant que li chiés soient copez; et c’est li muedre oevre, se li malaides n’a fievre et il est de chaude complexion.	And draw out blood from the sixth vein, just to the third; and if the artery is large, it is necessary that you tie it in two places with a strong silk thread, which does not allow any blood to come before the wound heals, and prevents clotting of blood; then remove the excess between the two threads in the same hour, and then, if you see, cauterize the wound with a cauterizing iron just up to the bone until the joints are covered; and this is the best work, if the pains are not fever and he is of hot constitution.
Car li cauteres est aide por finir les moistors: por ceu est il de plus grant aide as moistors.	For the fire cautery is to finish off the moistures: because it is the greatest help against moistures.
Ou il covient por l’estraction des arteres que om emplisse lou leu de viel coton et mette on sus tentes bien faites; et quant on les desliera, si soit curez de medicines seches que font naistre char, et de tentes, tant qu’il soit sanez; et se sans cort de l’artere tant dis com tu i oevres, si te haste dou coper par cautere, ou tu emple lou leu de vitriole et l’estrain a ta main que li sans soit estainchiez; et se tu n’as ceu present, si met sor le leu ton doit tant que li sans soit congelez, et arose le leu d’aigue froide tant que li sans cesse, et soit estraint si com il covient; et ceu qui est muedre et plus legier en l’estraction de l’artere est que tu cauterizes la voinne de cest cautere trenchant de II pars, mais li trenchant soient bien espés por warder plus longement lor chalor.	For the extraction of arteries, it is necessary to fill the limb with old cotton and place dry bandages on top; and when they are removed, care must be taken with dry medicines that make heat and bandages, as long as they are clean; and if there is no bleeding from the artery, as much as you can work, then hasten to cover it with a cauterizer, or fill the limb with vinegar and apply it to your hand that the wound is not stained; and if you do not have this present, then place ice on the limb until the wound is frozen, and raise the limb in cold water until it is constantly frozen, and it should be held as necessary; and what is more difficult and lighter in the extraction of the artery is that you cauterize the vein with this cauterizer cutting from II parts, but the cutting should be well spaced to last longer.
Car quant li estrumens est trop tenves, si tient moins sa chalor.	When instruments are too tight, they hold less heat.
Et doit avoir entre les II coutelz I doit de gros d’espaice, et puis quant tu as signiet d’enche les II leus, et tu mes lou fer ardant sus tant qu’il viegne jusc’a l’os, et cope la voinne en II leus; et soient esloigniet entre les II chiés car il n’est mie soudez de cest cautere dou tout en tout; et c’est li forme dou cautere:	And there should be between the two knives a large space, and then when you have signaled to insert the two blades, and you melt the hot iron as it approaches the bone, and cut the vein in two places; and they should be separated between the two wounds because it is not safe to use this cauterization throughout; and this is the form of the cauterization:
des larmes	of tears
Quant les larmes des eulz sont dessendans des voinnes que sont sus lou test dou chief de fuer, et il ne profite mie cure de medicine c’on i faice, et tu vois la faice dou malaide enrougir, et sent ou front ambulation si com de fremis; et sui oil sont tenve et moiste si que li poil des papieres sont cheut, et sont eschaufees les papieres, et escorchies de l’ardor des larmes, si ait mestier de ceste cure.	When the tears of the eyes are falling into the veins that are above the skin of the forehead, and it does not improve with medical treatment, and you see the face of the pain become twisted, and it feels as if it is quivering; and they are held tight and wet so that the hair of the scalp is burned, and the scalp is scorched by the heat of the tears, if necessary for this treatment.
